          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }
        .container-issue-content {
          padding: 0;
          flex-grow: 1;

          width: 100%;
          max-width: 100%;
          margin: auto;
          padding: 0;
          display: flex;
          align-items: stretch;

          flex-direction: row;
          flex-wrap: no-wrap;
        }

          padding: 0.5em 16px;

        }
        .metadata-container {
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);

          border-right: var(--chops-normal-border);

          width: 24em;
          min-width: 256px;
          flex-grow: 0;

        }

          margin-bottom: 0.25em;
          width: 100%;

          min-width: 50%;

          padding-right: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);

          position: sticky;
          overflow-y: auto;
          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }

          mr-issue-details, mr-launch-overview {
            width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

UserAgent: Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/99.0.4844.0 Safari/537.36



<span class="line"><!---->UserAgent: Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/99.0.4844.0 Safari/537.36<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Steps to reproduce the problem:



<span class="line"><!---->Steps to reproduce the problem:<!----></span>



<br>





#Reproduce



<span class="line"><!---->#Reproduce<!----></span>



<br>





The problem was found by my fuzzer running on CF(CC Security team for access permission 



<span class="line"><!---->The problem was found by my fuzzer running on CF(CC Security team for access permission <!----></span>





https://clusterfuzz.com/testcase-detail/6544221896769536



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://clusterfuzz.com/testcase-detail/6544221896769536"><!---->https://clusterfuzz.com/testcase-detail/6544221896769536<!----></a>





),



<span class="line"><!---->),<!----></span>



<br>





But because it cannot be reproduced stably, CF does not automatically report.



<span class="line"><!---->But because it cannot be reproduced stably, CF does not automatically report.<!----></span>



<br>





By manual review, it is found that the window time triggered by the vulnerability is very short, so it cannot be reproduced stably.



<span class="line"><!---->By manual review, it is found that the window time triggered by the vulnerability is very short, so it cannot be reproduced stably.<!----></span>



<br>





I will give a detailed vulnerability analysis later.



<span class="line"><!---->I will give a detailed vulnerability analysis later.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





What is the expected behavior?



<span class="line"><!---->What is the expected behavior?<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





What went wrong?



<span class="line"><!---->What went wrong?<!----></span>



<br>





Type of crash



<span class="line"><!---->Type of crash<!----></span>



<br>





render tab



<span class="line"><!---->render tab<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





#Analysis



<span class="line"><!---->#Analysis<!----></span>



<br>





The issue was introduced by CL(



<span class="line"><!---->The issue was introduced by CL(<!----></span>





https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/3472847



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/3472847"><!---->https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/3472847<!----></a>





)



<span class="line"><!---->)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1. PeerConnectionDependencyFactory is on-heap object, and there is a member WebrtcVideoPerfReporter is off-heap object.[3,4]



<span class="line"><!---->1. PeerConnectionDependencyFactory is on-heap object, and there is a member WebrtcVideoPerfReporter is off-heap object.[3,4]<!----></span>



<br>





2. When PeerConnectionDependencyFactory is constructed[2], the WebrtcVideoPerfReporter::Initialize will be called[1], 



<span class="line"><!---->2. When PeerConnectionDependencyFactory is constructed[2], the WebrtcVideoPerfReporter::Initialize will be called[1], <!----></span>



<br>





and eventually a new task will be created using WebrtcVideoPerfReporter's weak_this_ as this and post to task_runner_[1].



<span class="line"><!---->and eventually a new task will be created using WebrtcVideoPerfReporter's weak_this_ as this and post to task_runner_[1].<!----></span>



<br>





3. Because PeerConnectionDependencyFactory is an on-heap object, the destructor will not be called immediately when PeerConnectionDependencyFactory is GCed,



<span class="line"><!---->3. Because PeerConnectionDependencyFactory is an on-heap object, the destructor will not be called immediately when PeerConnectionDependencyFactory is GCed,<!----></span>



<br>





 so the weak_this_ of WebrtcVideoPerfReporter will not be reset, resulting in UAP.



<span class="line"><!----> so the weak_this_ of WebrtcVideoPerfReporter will not be reset, resulting in UAP.<!----></span>



<br>





4. PeerConnectionDependencyFactory uses CleanupPeerConnectionFactory to do some cleanup[5],



<span class="line"><!---->4. PeerConnectionDependencyFactory uses CleanupPeerConnectionFactory to do some cleanup[5],<!----></span>



<br>





so we can invalidate WebrtcVideoPerfReporter's weak_this_ here to fix the problem, I'll provide a patch ASAP.



<span class="line"><!---->so we can invalidate WebrtcVideoPerfReporter's weak_this_ here to fix the problem, I'll provide a patch ASAP.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>

so we can invalidate WebrtcVideoPerfReporter's weak_this_ here to fix the problem, I'll provide a patch ASAP.

Step 4-2. The thread invokes pre-finalizers. At this point, no destructors have been invoked. Thus the pre-finalizers are allowed to touch any other on-heap objects (which may get destructed in this sweeping phase).

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.
